        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer43452870" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10296508083725541354"><i>Ashes of Midnight</i> is the sixth in the Midnight Breed series and the books should be read in order because they continue solving a problem while each installment has a different hero/heroine. There are also brief updates on previous characters in later books. <br/><br/>The series has come a (very) long way since the first saga was told. Now the plot to get rid of the really bad guy (Dragos), hunt the Ancient, kill the Gen Ones (bad ones) and restore order to the vampire community is what keeps the series m</span>
  <span id="freeText10296508083725541354" style="display:none"><i>Ashes of Midnight</i> is the sixth in the Midnight Breed series and the books should be read in order because they continue solving a problem while each installment has a different hero/heroine. There are also brief updates on previous characters in later books. <br /><br />The series has come a (very) long way since the first saga was told. Now the plot to get rid of the really bad guy (Dragos), hunt the Ancient, kill the Gen Ones (bad ones) and restore order to the vampire community is what keeps the series moving along. Each book brings us closer to resolving the multitude of problems with a few turns and twists.<br /><br />Andreas is the hero, but his character was first introduced in earlier book(s). It is important to read #5 before #6 because a series of events and <i> Ashes of Midnight</i> picks up right where #5 left off. The heroine, Claire, is a new character and I enjoyed how the author wrote the couple's backstory. Nice twist. Claire and Andreas had a past and as the plot unfolds we learn who interfered with their love and why. The plot thickens...<br /><br />There were some excellent action scenes in this little book. Seems like the author may be trying to move out of the romance with steam into more action/fantasy with mentions of what happened behind the bedroom door. So unlike the earlier books in this series. <br /><br />Felt there was too much recapping of events already told, but overall I enjoyed the story, plot and characters. <br /><br />Being 50 does not make a person old in 2009...page 188. For shame! ;-)</span>
  <a data-text-id="10296508083725541354" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_222572531" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/222572531" />
    <a title="Denise ~The Procrastinating Book Diva~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4133839-denise-the-procrastinating-book-diva"><img alt="Denise ~The Procrastinating Book Diva~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603068275p2/4133839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/222572531?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Denise ~The Procrastinating Book Diva~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Denise ~The Procrastinating Book Diva~" href="/user/show/4133839-denise-the-procrastinating-book-diva">Denise ~The Procrastinating Book Diva~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4133839-denise-the-procrastinating-book-diva?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer222572531" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17382175007862198592"><br/><i>
  <b>First read March 2009 - rating: 3 stars<br/>Re-read March 2013 - rating: 3 stars</b>
</i><br/><br/>Not my favorite book of the series - then or now. It bothers me when a series starts out focusing on a core group of characters and then all of a sudden it goes off the rails by giving a secondary character their own book. I really liked Andreas Reichen in previous books but he and Claire's story, while littered with sweet and tender moments, never really resonated with me because they are only loosely tied to the Ord</span>
  <span id="freeText17382175007862198592" style="display:none"><br /><i>
  <b>First read March 2009 - rating: 3 stars<br />Re-read March 2013 - rating: 3 stars</b>
</i><br /><br />Not my favorite book of the series - then or now. It bothers me when a series starts out focusing on a core group of characters and then all of a sudden it goes off the rails by giving a secondary character their own book. I really liked Andreas Reichen in previous books but he and Claire's story, while littered with sweet and tender moments, never really resonated with me because they are only loosely tied to the Order. So although the book moved the story along nicely, this kind of out of left field storytelling annoys me, therefore, made it difficult for me to emotionally invest in it. <br /><br />Fortunately, <i>Ashes of Midnight's</i> saving grace, and one of the main reasons I keep coming back to this series, is its character diversity. Here the heroine is bi-racial; she joins two established primary African American characters. I enjoy diversity in fiction - the world is filled with tons of different people and I love when books reflect that. LA has not done anything new by incorporating different ethnic groups in her writing, however, she is one of the only authors with a best selling series that has placed them in leading roles. So kudos to her for that!!<br /><br />Unfortunately, the more of this series I read, the more I realize that it's simply not as good as I initially thought.....and a gaggle of characters every color of the rainbow couldn't change that. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17382175007862198592" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1579193051" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3575110751547667976">Breed Warrior Andreas<br/> Special ability: Pyrokinesis, setting himself on fire like a human torch <br/> Age: Around 300 years old <br/><br/>Breedmate Claire <br/> Special ability: Walking in the dreams of people<br/> Occupation: Musician, Composer <br/> Mark place: Right side of neck<br/><br/>Settings: Germany (Hamburg, countryside), Denmark, USA (Boston, Newport Rhodes island, Connecticut)<br/><br/>I had a small crash with Andreas at Tegan's book. He was the movie star handsome bad boy. I was looking forward to reading his story. I also liked Hel</span>
  <span id="freeText3575110751547667976" style="display:none">Breed Warrior Andreas<br /> Special ability: Pyrokinesis, setting himself on fire like a human torch <br /> Age: Around 300 years old <br /><br />Breedmate Claire <br /> Special ability: Walking in the dreams of people<br /> Occupation: Musician, Composer <br /> Mark place: Right side of neck<br /><br />Settings: Germany (Hamburg, countryside), Denmark, USA (Boston, Newport Rhodes island, Connecticut)<br /><br />I had a small crash with Andreas at Tegan's book. He was the movie star handsome bad boy. I was looking forward to reading his story. I also liked Helen which was his bloodhost. I was really sad with the outcome of their relationship.<br /><br />In this book Andreas is fighting to control his temper, his guilt, his power over his ability to create fire. He is really suffering in almost all the book. At least I am happy he is somewhat happy in the end.<br /><br />Claire was just ok. I found her a bit boring and I really could not understand her attitude when they split up with Andreas years ago. She just jumped from one vampire to the other in a very short time, the bastard Wilhelm Roth. Moreover, she did not act as a heartbroken woman all these years -only when she thought Andreas died and again she was too cold, not very convincing.<br /><br />Anyway, Andreas' story -and only his story- made the book great.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3575110751547667976" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17359266114908436552">I really like this series and even since meeting Andre I looked forward to his story. I engaged with his character and after the tragedy that happenned in his life, I wanted to see him find happiness again.<br/><br/>What didn't work for me was Claire. Could there ever be anyone so dumb and idiotic like her......the whole trust issue she had with Andre...please...where are you coming from???? I wanted to throttle her a few times.<br/><br/>Loved getting to see the characters from the previous books...Lucan & Gabriell</span>
  <span id="freeText17359266114908436552" style="display:none">I really like this series and even since meeting Andre I looked forward to his story. I engaged with his character and after the tragedy that happenned in his life, I wanted to see him find happiness again.<br /><br />What didn't work for me was Claire. Could there ever be anyone so dumb and idiotic like her......the whole trust issue she had with Andre...please...where are you coming from???? I wanted to throttle her a few times.<br /><br />Loved getting to see the characters from the previous books...Lucan &amp; Gabrielle...I love that couple and Mira...adore her...not forgetting Renata...what great characters.<br /><br />World building continues to grow and I can't wait for the next story.</span>

<div id="review_2916248162" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2916248162" />
    <a title="Crissy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13992033-crissy"><img alt="Crissy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1507251486p2/13992033.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Crissy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Crissy" href="/user/show/13992033-crissy">Crissy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2916248162" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16700874169872609450">I listened to the audible version of the story and it was a good paranormal romance. Claire is a breedmate and bonded to Wilhelm but Claire and Reichen have a past and a love for each other that will never die. Reichen is seeking revenge and nothing will stop him from getting to Wilhelm, not even Claire. This was a non-stop action story that did not disappoint and left me wanting the next book in the series. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jPVtxEI+axxU43yWr9ZZhflRC1vklMUZhZjWJL3GUqyT1OuQzfOa8qNli+89+fnxGLgzE+jsFz/AN5k4SMdPPg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('r3XOlc6tEEitU8o/VhmatIo5EPmFy1N0oVuT9MZIISOwVEjBQWDhplrVPUbENjrAa9AosYmzgVLk9NzoM0k8sQ==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer17380048106985860090"><b>LARA ADRIAN</b> is a <i>New York Times</i> and #1 internationally best-selling author with nearly 4 million books in print and digital worldwide and translations licensed to more than 20 countries. Her books have been named among Amazon’s Top Ten Romances of the Year, and have also been nominated by readers multiple times as finalists for the Goodreads Choice Award for Best Romance of the Year. Reviewers hav</span>
  <span id="freeText17380048106985860090" style="display:none"><b>LARA ADRIAN</b> is a <i>New York Times</i> and #1 internationally best-selling author with nearly 4 million books in print and digital worldwide and translations licensed to more than 20 countries. Her books have been named among Amazon’s Top Ten Romances of the Year, and have also been nominated by readers multiple times as finalists for the Goodreads Choice Award for Best Romance of the Year. Reviewers have called Lara’s books “addictively readable” (Chicago Tribune), “extraordinary” (Fresh Fiction), “strikingly original” (Booklist), and “one of the best vampire series on the market” (Romantic Times).<br /> <br />Writing as <b>TINA ST. JOHN</b>, her historical romances have won numerous awards including the National Readers Choice; Romantic Times Magazine Reviewer’s Choice; Booksellers Best; and many others. She was twice named a Finalist in Romance Writers of America’s RITA Awards, for Best Historical Romance (White Lion’s Lady) and Best Paranormal Romance (Heart of the Hunter). More recently, the German translation of Heart of the Hunter debuted on Der Spiegel bestseller list.<br /><br />With an ancestry stretching back to the Mayflower and the court of King Henry VIII, the author lives with her husband in New England, where she is working on her next novel. Visit Lara’s website and sign up for new release announcements at <a href="http://bit.ly/LaraAdrianNews" rel="nofollow noopener">http://bit.ly/LaraAdrianNews</a><br /></span>
